Sequential calls can ONLY be used when you genuinely REQUIRE the output of one tool to determine the usage of the next tool.\n\nDEFAULT TO PARALLEL: Unless you have a specific reason why operations MUST be sequential (output of A required for input of B), always execute multiple tools simultaneously. This is not just an optimization - it's the expected behavior. authentication schemes\n- **Core component attribute definitions**: When describing properties, types, default values, and behaviors of key UI components, services, or configuration objects\n- **Database table schemas**: When outlining tables, columns, data types, constraints (PK, FK, unique), indexes, and relationships between entities\n- **Configuration options**: When listing environment variables, feature flags, or system settings with descriptions, valid values, and scope\n- **State or enum definitions**: When clarifying possible states, status codes, or enumerated values used across the system\n- **Input/output specifications**: When defining the structure of data inputs (forms, payloads) or expected outputs (reports, responses) for clarity and validation\n- **Migration or version changes**: When comparing changes across versions, such as deprecated fields, added endpoints, or schema evolution\n\n## 7. Error\"]\n    DBResult --\u003e|Yes| ProcessData[\"Process Raw Data\"]\n    ProcessData --\u003e UpdateCache[\"Update Cache\"]\n    UpdateCache --\u003e ReturnResult[\"Return Processed Result\"]\n    HandleError --\u003e ReturnError\n    ReturnCache --\u003e End([Function Exit])\n    ReturnResult --\u003e End\n    ReturnError --\u003e End\n```\n\n## Architecture Diagrams\n```mermaid\ngraph TB\n uuid id PK\n    string name\n    string description\n    uuid owner_id FK\n    timestamp created_at\n    timestamp updated_at\n    enum status\n  }\n\n  TASK {\n    uuid id PK\n    string title\n    text description\n    uuid project_id FK\n    uuid assignee_id FK\n    timestamp due_date\n    enum priority\n    enum status\n  }\n\n  USER ||--o{ PROJECT : owns\n  USER ||--o{ TASK : assigned_to\n  PROJECT ||--o{ TASK : contains\n```\n\n## Common Mermaid Syntax Errors to Avoid:\n\n### WRONG - Custom Colors and Styling\n```\nclassDiagram\n    class User {\n        name: string\n    }\n  A[Complex Label With Spaces] --\u003e B\n```\n\n### CORRECT - Quoted Labels\n```mermaid\nflowchart TD\n    A[\"Complex Label With Spaces\"] --\u003e B[\"Another Label\"]\n```\n\n# FINAL DOCUMENT Confirm that the data includes the activities property for the Syrian Community card.\n- Hover effects not applying\n  - Confirm that the custom color tokens and Tailwind theme are configured and that the component applies the intended hover classes.\n- Decorative assets visibility\n  - Verify that the decorative eagle assets are accessible and sized appropriately for the background overlay.\n- Responsive layout expectations\n  - On small screens, the logo and text stack vertically within each card. If layout appears off, review Tailwind breakpoint classes and container widths.\n\n**Section sources**\n- [LanguageContext.tsx](file://src/contexts/LanguageContext.tsx#L1-L292)\n- [OrganizersSection.tsx](file://src/components/OrganizersSection.tsx#L1-L132)\n- [index.css](file://src/index.css#L55-L163)\n- [tailwind.config.ts](file://src/tailwind.config.ts#L44-L84)\n\n## Conclusion\nThe OrganizersSection component provides a clean, multilingual presentation of organizing institutions with a two-tier card layout.
